<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:moraal.html>moraal</a> (6220)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">moral</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mōrālis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">relating to manners or morals</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
(first used by <a href = vnd.unilang:cicero.html>Cicero</a>, to translate Ancient Greek <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἠθικός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ēthikós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">moral</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:mos.html>mos</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">manner, custom</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***morbide.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:morbide.html>morbide</a> (16222)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:morbide.html>morbide</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">morbidus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:morbide.html>morbide</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:morn.html>morn</a> (90509)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">mōrn</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">morwen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>morgen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*murganaz</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*murginaz</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">moarn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>Morgen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>morgen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>Morgen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>morgen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">morgon</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mr̥kéno</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mr̥kóno</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*Mr̥Hko</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy"><a href = vnd.unilang:boren.html>bore</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">mérkti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to blink, <a href = vnd.unilang:twinkle.html>twinkle</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">मरीचि</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">márīci</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:ray.html>ray</a> of light</span><span class="polytonic mention" lang="el">μέρα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">méra</span>, <span <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:morn.html>morn</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">morns</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now  poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Morning.
<ul><li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Hamlet" class="extiw" title="s:Hamlet"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamlet.html>Hamlet</a></a></i>, lines 165-168,
<dl><dd>But look, the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:morn.html>morn</a></b>, in russet <a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a> clad, / Walks <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> the dew of yon high eastward hill. / Break <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> our watch up, and by my advice, / Let us impart what <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> have seen tonight</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> morning (1016)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:morsen.html>morsen</a> (19600)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Germanic, from <a href = vnd.unilang:mors.html>mors</a>(ch) 'weak, soft dirt' (which <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> less obscure homonyms)
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:morsen.html>morsen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To spill, drop something, especially mindlessly and/or so that it spreads out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To be dirty or be occupied with soil, make a mess</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To conceal, hide something</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To sketch, make a test draw</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bemorsen</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">ontmorsen</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">uitmorsen</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">vermorsen</span> (verbs)</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">morserd</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mortier.html>mortier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:mortier.html>mortier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mortārium</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mos.html>mos</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:mos.html>mos</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*musą</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mosterd.html>mosterd</a> (7942)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mostaert</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">moustarde</i> (French: <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">moutarde</i>), from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">moust</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">must</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mustum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mosterd.html>mosterd</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mosterd.html>mosterds</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mosterd.html>mosterdje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>mustard</li></ol>

***mot.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mot.html>mot</a> (12071)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:motten.html>motte</a></i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">moth</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:motten.html>Motte</a></i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

***motel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:motel.html>motel</a> (3313)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Motel%26TV%28byNotSteve%29.jpg/220px-Motel%26TV%28byNotSteve%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Motel%26TV%28byNotSteve%29.jpg/330px-Motel%26TV%28byNotSteve%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Motel%26TV%28byNotSteve%29.jpg/440px-Motel%26TV%28byNotSteve%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1545" data-file-height="1024" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>A <b><a href = vnd.unilang:motel.html>motel</a></b> sign</div></div></div>
<p>Blend of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:motor.html>motor</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hotel.html>hotel</a></i>, from the original <a href = vnd.unilang:motel.html>Motel</a> Inn of San <a href = vnd.unilang:luis.html>Luis</a> Obispo in California, USA, established in 1925 by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arthur_Heineman" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Arthur Heineman">Arthur Heineman</a> (1878–1974).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:motel.html>motel</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:motels.html>motels</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also  attributive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A type of <a href = vnd.unilang:hotel.html>hotel</a> or lodging establishment, often located near a major highway, which typically features a series of <a href = vnd.unilang:rooms.html>rooms</a> the entrances of which are immediately adjacent to a parking lot to facilitate convenient access to automobiles parked there.</li>
<li>A low-cost short-stay <a href = vnd.unilang:hotel.html>hotel</a>, often with hourly rates rather than daily rates, and notorious for permitting illicit sexual activities; love <a href = vnd.unilang:hotel.html>hotel</a>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:hotel.html>hotel</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> See also Thesaurus:lodging place</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">love <a href = vnd.unilang:hotel.html>hotel</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> See also Thesaurus:love <a href = vnd.unilang:hotel.html>hotel</a></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:motel.html>motel</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:motels.html>motels</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">moteling</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">motelling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">moteled</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">motelled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To stay in a <a href = vnd.unilang:motel.html>motel</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:motels.html>motels</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:motie.html>motie</a> (11025)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***motief.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:motief.html>motief</a> (3415)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">motijf</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">motif</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mōtīvus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:motief.html>motief</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:motieven.html>motieven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:motiefje.html>motiefje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A motive.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:motief.html>motief</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moord.html>moord</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:misdaden.html>misdaden</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> carrière, <a href = vnd.unilang:zelfs.html>zelfs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:relatie.html>relaties</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alleen.html>alleen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:poen.html>poen</a>, doekoe, <a href = vnd.unilang:pegels.html>pegels</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ja.html>ja</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>geld</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>geld</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>geld</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>motive</b> for the murder, her other crimes, her career, <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> all of her relations <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> nothing but moolah, <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>jack</a>, spondulicks, yes money, money, money.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelegenheid.html>gelegenheid</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:motief.html>motief</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>He <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> the opportunity, but no <b>motive</b>.<i></i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">art<span class="ib-comma">,</span> music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A motif, a pattern.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:motief.html>motief</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:komt.html>komt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:acht.html>acht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:keer.html>keer</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opera.html>opera</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><i>That <b>motif</b> occurs eight times in this <a href = vnd.unilang:opera.html>opera</a>.</i></dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stof.html>stof</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:motief.html>motief</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bestaat.html>bestaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vierkantjes.html>vierkantjes</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><i>This fabric <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a <b>motif</b> consisting of little <a href = vnd.unilang:squares.html>squares</a>.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

***motor.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:motor.html>motor</a> (1559)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:motor.html>motor</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:motor.html>motor</a></i>. In the sense “motorbike” <i><a href = vnd.unilang:motor.html>motor</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> originally short for <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">motorrijwiel</i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:motorfiets.html>motorfiets</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_9">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:motor.html>motor</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:motoren.html>motoren</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">motors</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:motortje.html>motortje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>engine (mechanical device)</li>
<li>motorbike
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:motorfiets.html>motorfiets</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">motorrijwiel</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***moussaka.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:moussaka.html>moussaka</a> (60008)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Greek language">Greek</a></span> <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">μουσακάς</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mousakás</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">musakka</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">مُسَقَّعَة</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">musaqqaʿa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chilled</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:moussaka.html>moussaka</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">moussakas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A dish consisting of layers of minced lamb or beef, sliced <a href = vnd.unilang:aubergine.html>aubergine</a> (eggplant) or potatoes, tomatoes and béchamel sauce, baked in the <a href = vnd.unilang:oven.html>oven</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:moussaka.html>moussaka</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

***mout.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mout.html>mout</a> (81290)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">malt</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mout.html>mout</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">malt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*maltą</i>.
</p>
